OBJECT Report 14000713 Sales Shipment Invoice
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=12/28/17;
    Time=12:00:00 PM;
    Version List=SE0.60.18;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Sales Shipment Invoice;
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  SalesShipmentLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.","Order Line No.");
                  PackingStation.GetPackingStation;
                  CLEAR(CompanyAddress);
                  EShipFormatAddr.PackingStation(CompanyAddress,PackingStation);
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 5581;    ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table112;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               ReqFilterHeadingML=ENU=Sales Invoice;
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalesInvLine@1240030000 : Record 113;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF "Salesperson Code" = '' THEN
                                    CLEAR(SalesPurchPerson)
                                  ELSE
                                    SalesPurchPerson.GET("Salesperson Code");

                                  FormatAddress.SalesInvBillTo(BillToAddress,"Sales Invoice Header");
                                  FormatAddress.SalesInvShipTo(ShipToAddress,CustAddress,"Sales Invoice Header");

                                  IF "Payment Terms Code" = '' THEN
                                    CLEAR(PaymentTerms)
                                  ELSE
                                    PaymentTerms.GET("Payment Terms Code");

                                  IF "Shipment Method Code" = '' THEN
                                    CLEAR(ShipmentMethod)
                                  ELSE
                                    ShipmentMethod.GET("Shipment Method Code");

                                  Customer.GET("Bill-to Customer No.");

                                  ShippingCharge := 0;
                                  SalesInvLine.RESET;
                                  SalesInvLine.SETRANGE("Document No.","No.");
                                  SalesInvLine.SETRANGE("Shipping Charge",TRUE);
                                  IF SalesInvLine.FIND('-') THEN
                                    REPEAT
                                      ShippingCharge := ShippingCharge + SalesInvLine.Amount + SalesInvLine."Inv. Discount Amount";
                                    UNTIL SalesInvLine.NEXT = 0;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Sell-to Customer No.,Bill-to Customer No.,Ship-to Code,No. Printed }

    { 8703;1   ;Column  ;Sales_Invoice_Header_No_;
               SourceExpr="No." }

    { 5701;1   ;DataItem;CopyLoop            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               NoLoops := 1 + ABS(NoCopies) + Customer."Invoice Copies";
                               IF NoLoops <= 0 THEN
                                 NoLoops := 1;
                               CopyNo := 0;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CurrReport.PAGENO := 1;

                                  IF CopyNo = NoLoops THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN
                                      SalesInvPrinted.RUN("Sales Invoice Header");
                                    CurrReport.BREAK;
                                  END ELSE
                                    CopyNo := CopyNo + 1;
                                  IF CopyNo = 1 THEN // Original
                                    CLEAR(CopyTxt)
                                  ELSE
                                    CopyTxt := 'COPY';
                                END;
                                 }

    { 6455;2   ;DataItem;PageLoop            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1570;3   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table113;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.)
                                 WHERE(Shipping Charge=FILTER(No));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(TaxLiable,AmountExclInvDisc,Amount,"Amount Including VAT");
                               NumberOfLines := COUNT;
                               OnLineNumber := 0;
                               PrintFooter := FALSE;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  OnLineNumber := OnLineNumber + 1;

                                  OrderedQuantity :=  0;
                                  IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Order No." = '' THEN
                                    OrderedQuantity := Quantity
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                     IF SalesLine.GET(1,"Sales Invoice Header"."Order No.","Line No.") THEN
                                        OrderedQuantity := SalesLine.Quantity
                                     ELSE BEGIN
                                        SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order No.","Sales Invoice Header"."Order No.");
                                        SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order Line No.","Line No.");
                                        IF SalesShipmentLine.FIND('-') THEN;
                                        REPEAT
                                          OrderedQuantity := OrderedQuantity + SalesShipmentLine.Quantity;
                                        UNTIL 0=SalesShipmentLine.NEXT;
                                     END;
                                  END;

                                  DescriptionToPrint := Description;
                                  IF Type = 0 THEN BEGIN
                                    IF OnLineNumber < NumberOfLines THEN BEGIN
                                      NEXT;
                                      IF Type = 0 THEN BEGIN
                                        DescriptionToPrint := COPYSTR(DescriptionToPrint + ' ' + Description,1,MAXSTRLEN(DescriptionToPrint));
                                        OnLineNumber := OnLineNumber + 1;
                                      END ELSE
                                        NEXT(-1);
                                    END;
                                    "No." := '';
                                    "Unit of Measure" := '';
                                    Amount := 0;
                                    "Amount Including VAT" := 0;
                                    "Inv. Discount Amount" := 0;
                                    Quantity := 0;
                                  END ELSE IF Type = Type::"G/L Account" THEN
                                    "No." := '';

                                  IF "No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                                    HighDescriptionToPrint := DescriptionToPrint;
                                    LowDescriptionToPrint := '';
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    HighDescriptionToPrint := '';
                                    LowDescriptionToPrint := DescriptionToPrint;
                                  END;

                                  IF Amount <> "Amount Including VAT" THEN BEGIN
                                    TaxFlag := TRUE;
                                    TaxLiable := Amount;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    TaxFlag := FALSE;
                                    TaxLiable := 0;
                                  END;

                                  AmountExclInvDisc := Amount + "Inv. Discount Amount";

                                  IF Quantity = 0 THEN
                                    UnitPriceToPrint := 0  // so it won't print
                                  ELSE
                                    UnitPriceToPrint := ROUND(AmountExclInvDisc / Quantity,0.00001);
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Sales Invoice Header;
               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
